country_event = {
	id = kirin.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.1"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { ## Set Game Rules
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = KIR_ai_behavior
							option = HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
						}
						AND = {
							is_historical_focus_on = yes
							NOT = {
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = KIR_ai_behavior
									option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = KIR_ai_behavior
									option = NEUTRAL
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = KIR_ai_behavior
									option = COMMUNIST
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = KIR_ai_behavior
									option = RISING_SUN
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = KIR_ai_behavior
									option = FASCISM
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_GGO_SUCCESS
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = NEUTRAL
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = COMMUNIST
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
				KIC = { set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = RISING_SUN
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
				KIC = { set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = FASCISM
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = KIR_ai_behavior
						option = RANDOM
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_GGO_SUCCESS
					}
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
					}
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
					}
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
						KIC = { set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST }
					}
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
						KIC = { set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN }
					}
					1 = {
						set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = kirin.1.t
	desc = kirin.1.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_palace

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				is_ai = no
				has_country_flag = KIR_CIVIL_WAR_SCRIPTED_GAME_RULE
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin.1.a
		set_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_disabled_ideas_var value = 0 }
		add_political_power = 70
		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_available
		add_ideas =  KIR_pol_1
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_silence_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_stabilityWeeklyX_tt
		set_variable = { var = KIR_the_silence_weekly_stability_var value = -0.01 }
	}
}

		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_TIME_VAR_WEEKS = 183 }

		set_variable = { ImageY = -348 } #12
		set_variable = { TitleX = 200 }
		set_variable = { TitleY = -378 } #-18
		set_variable = { DescriptionX = 200 }
		set_variable = { DescriptionY = -342 } #18
		set_variable = { Description2X = 10 }
		set_variable = { Description2Y = -262 } #98
		set_variable = { Bar1TitleX = 50 }
		set_variable = { Bar1TitleY = -95 } #265
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_PROG_BARX = 38 }
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_PROG_BARY = -58 } #302
		set_variable = { Frame1X = 30 }
		set_variable = { Frame1Y = -65 } #295
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_PROG_NUMX = 30 }
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_PROG_NUMY = -65 } #295
		set_variable = { Bar2TitleX = 50 }
		set_variable = { Bar2TitleY = -16 } #344
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_TIME_BARX = 38 }
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_TIME_BARY = 17 } #377
		set_variable = { Frame2X = 30 }
		set_variable = { Frame2Y = 10 } #370
		set_variable = { KIR_GGO_TIME_NUMX = 30 }

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.10"}
	title = kirin.10.t
	desc = kirin.10.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_stamp

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				is_ai = no
				has_country_flag = KIR_CIVIL_WAR_SCRIPTED_GAME_RULE
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_event_10_DANGER_tt
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communism
			long_name = KIR_communism_party_1_long
			name = KIR_communism_party_1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_silence_stability1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_stab_var value = 0.01 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_communist1_tt
		#custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_shuffle_pol_advisors_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = KIR_pol_4
		set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_available
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0.1 }
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_2_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_3_removable
			set_country_flag = KIR_pol_4_removable
		}
		set_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kirin_utility.48 days = 120 random_days = 730 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
					has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_autumn_blaze
		set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_protag = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_entry  = 3 }
		KIR_diary_add_entry_to_protagonist = yes
		set_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_TRIUMVIRATE
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_NONALIGNED
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_COMMUNIST
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_RISING_SUN
						has_country_flag = KIR_PATH_SUPREMACIST
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kirin_utility.48 days = 120 random_days = 730 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

			add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0.1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin.307
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.307"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			DEL = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					teleport_armies = { limit = { always = yes } }
					add_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { unplanned_offensive }
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = KIR_DEL_Resistance
				country_event = { id = kirin.3700 hours = 1 }
				set_technology = { tech_support = 1 popup = no }
				load_oob = "KIR_DEL_Force"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					DEL = {
						is_in_faction = yes
					}
				}
				DEL = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = {
								is_in_faction_with = DEL
							}
							set_country_flag = DEL_FSW_Faction_Leader_Before
						}
					}
					else = {
						faction_leader = {
							set_country_flag = DEL_FSW_Faction_Leader_Before
						}
					}
					leave_faction = yes
					set_country_flag = DEL_FSW_Left_Faction
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					KIR = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				KIR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = DEL
						type = topple_government
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					DEL = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				DEL = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = KIR
						type = take_core_state
					}
				}
				KIR = {
					add_war_support = -0.1
					add_stability = -0.1
				}
			}
			else = {
				KIR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = DEL
						type = topple_government
					}
				}
			}
			KIR = {
				country_event = { id = kirin.308 days = 5 }
				add_war_support = 0.15
				set_country_flag = KIR_unlocked_SSVC_Company
				load_oob = "KIR_SSVC_Force"
				goto_province = 15947
			}
		}
	}
	title = kirin.307.t
	desc = kirin.307.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_festival

	is_triggered_only = yes

		DEL = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
	}

		set_country_flag = KIR_FS_WAR_Flag

					KIR = { has_country_flag = KIR_created_FSA_flag }
					FSA = { exists = yes }
				}
				FSA = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = KIR_SET
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						long_name = KIR_neutrality_party_DEL_SET_long
						name = KIR_neutrality_party_DEL_SET
					}
					KIR = {
						KIR_SSVC_presidency = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						character = "KIR_SSVC_presidency"
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							desc = ""
							ideology = libertarianism
							expire = "1965.1.1.1"
							traits = {  }
						}
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.1
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 1139
							state = 1141
							state = 1142
							state = 1144
							state = 1145
							state = 1192
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = KIR
							AND = {
								owner = {
									is_subject_of = KIR
								}
								controller = {
									is_subject_of = KIR
								}
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = FSA
					remove_claim_by = FSA
					add_core_of = FSA
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = KIR
					set_country_flag = KIR_FSA_flag
					KIR = {
						PREV = {
							transfer_technology = yes
							transfer_society_ideas = yes
							transfer_science_ideas = yes
							transfer_illiteracy_ideas = yes
							transfer_poverty_ideas = yes
						}
					}
					every_core_state = {
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 1139
								state = 1141
								state = 1142
								state = 1144
								state = 1145
								state = 1192
							}
							OR = {
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = KIR
								AND = {
									owner = {
										is_subject_of = KIR
									}
									controller = {
										is_subject_of = KIR
									}
								}
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = PREV
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism
						long_name = KIR_fascism_party_DEL_long
						name = KIR_fascism_party_DEL
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						long_name = KIR_neutrality_party_DEL_SET_long
						name = KIR_neutrality_party_DEL_SET
					}
					KIR = {
						puppet = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = KIR_SET
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 34
						neutrality = 41
						fascism = 22
						communism = 3
					}
					KIR = {
						KIR_SSVC_presidency = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						character = "KIR_SSVC_presidency"
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							desc = ""
							ideology = libertarianism
							expire = "1965.1.1.1"
							traits = {  }
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = blank_focus_tree
					reserve_dynamic_country = yes
					set_AI_strategies_on_every_possible_country_delayed = yes
					country_event = { id = kirin_utility.43 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin_utility.44 days = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_FSW_Internment_Camps
				}
				country_event = { id = kirin.334 days = 100 random_days = 265 }
			}
		}
	}
	title = kirin.350.t
	desc = kirin.350.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_palace

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kirin.350.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_political_power = 150
		if = {
			limit = {
				KIR = { has_country_flag = KIR_created_FSA_flag }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_event_350a_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_event_350_tt
		}
		FSA = {
			add_country_leader_trait = KIR_board_of_governors
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = thunder_tiger_nuked }
				}
				add_ideas = golden_city
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = thunder_tiger_nuked
				}
				add_ideas = golden_city_ruined
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1139 }
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1141 }
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1142 }
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1144 }
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1145 }
			give_resource_rights = { receiver = KIR state = 1192 }
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = kirin.106 ##Republic of Kiria declares war
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin.106"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					KIC = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				KIC = {
					declare_war_on = { ## The Kirian Revolution
						target = KIR
						type = liberate_wargoal
					}
					#add_civil_war_target = KIR ##These stop the scripted Peace of Massicot white peace from working
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					KIR = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				KIR = {
					declare_war_on = { ## The Western Secession
						target = KIC
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				KIR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = KIC
						type = annex_everything
					}
					#add_civil_war_target = KIC
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin.107 days = 30 random_days = 90 }
		}
	}
	title = kirin.106.t
	desc = kirin.106.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_cityfall

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kirin.106.a
		trigger = {
			original_tag = KIC
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		effect_tooltip = {
			KIC = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KIR
					type = liberate_wargoal
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			KIR = {
				news_event = { id = kirin_republic.2 days = 5 }
			}
			KIS = {
				news_event = { id = kirin_republic.2 days = 5 }
			}
			KIC = {
				news_event = { id = kirin_republic.2 days = 5 }
				country_event = { id = kirin_republic.55 days = 30 random_days = 90 }
				country_event = { id = kirin_republic.555 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin.106.b
		trigger = {
			original_tag = KIR
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			KIR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KIC
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = kirin.113.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_event_113_tt
		set_country_flag = KIR_FACTORY_SG_enabled
		##Option 1 (default) - 3:2:1
		#set_variable = { KIR_ratio_unit_var = 6 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 3 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		##Option 2 - 2:2:1
		#set_variable = { KIR_ratio_unit_var = 5 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		##Option 3 - 1:3:1
		#set_variable = { KIR_ratio_unit_var = 5 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 3 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		##Option 4 - 2:1:1
		#set_variable = { KIR_ratio_unit_var = 4 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		##Total Amount of Industry
		set_variable = { KIR_total_factories_count_var = KIR.num_of_civilian_factories }
		add_to_variable = { KIR_total_factories_count_var = KIR.num_of_military_factories }
		add_to_variable = { KIR_total_factories_count_var = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
		##A Unit of Industry - yardstick by which the ratio is measured
		#set_variable = { KIR_ratio_of_factories_var = KIR.KIR_total_factories_count_var }
		#divide_variable = { KIR_ratio_of_factories_var = KIR.KIR_ratio_unit_var }
		set_variable = { KIR_ratio_of_factories_var = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
		##Ratio of Civilian Factories
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio = KIR.num_of_civilian_factories }
		divide_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio = KIR.KIR_ratio_of_factories_var }
		##Ratio of Military Factories
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio = KIR.num_of_military_factories }
		divide_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio = KIR.KIR_ratio_of_factories_var }
		##Ratio of Naval Factories
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
		divide_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio = KIR.KIR_ratio_of_factories_var }
		##Set Frames
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_1_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_2_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_3_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_4_frame = 1 }
		##Starting off with 2:2:1 ratio
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_2_frame = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_3_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_1_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_4_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		##Starting off with 3:2:1 ratio
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_2_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_3_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_1_frame = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_RATIO_OPTION_4_frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat = 3 }
		set_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat = 2 }
		set_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_ratio_flat = 1 }
		set_variable = { KIR_MIL_FAC_PP_COST = 50 }
		##Get Factory Ratio
		KIR_get_factory_ratio = yes
	}
}

				show_mio_tooltip = KIS_guild_artificer_organization
				mio:KIS_guild_artificer_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
					add_mio_funds = 400
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer_individual
				show_ideas_tooltip = KIS_guild_artificer
			}
		}
	}
}

			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_neutrality_var value = 0.05 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_crisis.15.b
		add_political_power = -50
		set_variable = { var = KIR_develop_1059_decision_cost_var value = 25 }
		unlock_decision_tooltip = develop_vermilion_basin_crystals
		unlock_decision_tooltip = develop_vermilion_basin_tungsten
		set_country_flag = KIR_can_develop_vermilion_basin_crystals
		set_country_flag = KIR_can_develop_vermilion_basin_tungsten
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_crisis.15.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIR_plenum_dynamic_modifier }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_modify_plenum_communist2_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { var = KIR_plenum_communism_var value = 0.05 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		set_variable = { var = KIR_develop_1059_decision_cost_var value = 50 }
		unlock_decision_tooltip = develop_vermilion_basin_crystals
		unlock_decision_tooltip = develop_vermilion_basin_tungsten
		set_country_flag = KIR_can_develop_vermilion_basin_crystals
		set_country_flag = KIR_can_develop_vermilion_basin_tungsten
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_event_15_option_c_tt
		set_country_flag = KIR_event_15_resources_decisions_nerfed
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_loyalists.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_loyalists.7"}
	title = kirin_loyalists.7.t
	desc = kirin_loyalists.7.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_city

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.7.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_thunderbolts_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 1064
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					}
					set_technology = {
						aa_lmg = 1
						engines_1 = 1
						engines_2 = 1
						early_bombs = 1
						aircraft_construction = 1
						iw_small_airframe = 1
						iw_medium_airframe = 1
						iw_large_airframe = 1
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Hollow Shades Demon"
						type = small_plane_airframe_0
						modules = {
							fixed_main_weapon_slot = light_mg_2x
							engine_type_slot = engine_1_1x
							special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
						}
						icon = "GFX_ENG_light_plane_5_medium"
						obsolete = yes
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Breezie Gordon"
						type = small_plane_cas_airframe_0
						modules = {
							fixed_main_weapon_slot = bomb_locks
							engine_type_slot = engine_1_1x
							special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
						}
						icon = "GFX_ENG_CAS1_medium"
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Handley Page Hayford"
						type = medium_plane_airframe_0
						modules = {
							fixed_main_weapon_slot = medium_bomb_bay
							engine_type_slot = engine_1_2x
							special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
						}
					}
					load_oob = "KIR_thunderbolts_bba"
				}
				else = {
					set_technology = {
						early_fighter = 1
						early_bomber = 1
					}
					load_oob = "KIR_thunderbolts"
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					has_tech = iw_small_airframe
				}
				generic_early_fighter = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_1
					variant_name = "Basic Fighter"
					amount = 40
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					NOT = {
						has_tech = iw_small_airframe
					}
				}
				set_technology = {
					iw_small_airframe = 1
				}
				generic_early_fighter = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_1
					variant_name = "Early Fighter"
					amount = 40
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = early_fighter
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe
					amount = 40
					producer = EQS
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_technology = {
					early_fighter = 1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe
					amount = 40
					producer = EQS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"
				}
				add_equipment_subsidy = {
					cic = 250
					equipment_type = small_plane_airframe
					seller_tags = { EQS CRY NLR VAN SCS LSP NMS CES JUN BAL TEM BUF }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
				}
				generic_early_tac_bomber = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_plane_airframe_0
					variant_name = "Early Tactical Bomber"
					amount = 20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					NOT = {
						has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
					}
				}
				set_technology = {
					iw_medium_airframe = 1
				}
				generic_early_tac_bomber = yes
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_plane_airframe_0
					variant_name = "Early Tactical Bomber"
					amount = 20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = early_bomber
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_plane_airframe
					amount = 20
					producer = EQS
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_technology = {
					early_bomber = 1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_plane_airframe
					amount = 20
					producer = EQS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}
				add_equipment_subsidy = {

					equipment_type = medium_plane_airframe

country_event = {
	id = kirin_loyalists.26 ##Nirik Collapse - figure out how to deal with advisors.
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_loyalists.26"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = KIR_Triumvirate_Collapsed_Flag
			set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_communism_popularity_var = party_popularity@communism }
			set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_democratic_popularity_var = party_popularity@democratic }
			set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_neutrality_popularity_var = party_popularity@neutrality }
			multiply_variable = { KIR_preCWII_communism_popularity_var = 21 }
			multiply_variable = { KIR_preCWII_democratic_popularity_var = 21 }
			multiply_variable = { KIR_preCWII_neutrality_popularity_var = 21 }
			set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_population_loss_var = 192000 } ##roughly the total marepower of nirik bands
			divide_variable = { KIR_preCWII_population_loss_var = KIR.num_controlled_states }
			set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_population_loss_NEGATIVE_var = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { KIR_preCWII_population_loss_NEGATIVE_var = KIR_preCWII_population_loss_var }
			save_current_manpower = yes
			every_controlled_state = {
				add_manpower = KIR.KIR_preCWII_population_loss_NEGATIVE_var
			}
			restore_previous_manpower = yes
			every_controlled_state = {
				set_variable = { KIR_preCWII_kill_infra_var = infrastructure_level }
				divide_variable = { KIR_preCWII_kill_infra_var = 2 }
				remove_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = KIR_preCWII_kill_infra_var
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				popup = no
				KIR_irregular_tech = 1
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Nirik Band"
				template_counter = 84
				regiments = {
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					kirin_braves = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					kirin_braves = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
					owner = ROOT
					count = 21
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no
				}
				set_state_flag = KIR_civil_war_meltdown_capital_state_flag
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = KIR
				save_event_target_as = KIR_autumn_blaze_breakaway
				set_country_flag = KIR_autumn_blaze_breakaway_flag
				transfer_state = 1080
				set_capital = {
					state = 1080
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 0
					neutrality = 0
					fascism = 100
					communism = 0
				}
				set_technology = {
					melee_weapons = 1
					melee_weapons1 = 1
					pre_gw_artillery = 1
					kirin_race = 1
					tech_kirin_vanguard = 1
					tech_kirin_vanguard2 = 1
					tech_kirin_vanguard3 = 1
					tech_kirin_brave = 1
					tech_kirin_brave2 = 1
					tech_kirin_brave3 = 1

				every_controlled_state = {
					add_core_of = KWF
				}
			}
			KRS = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					add_core_of = KRS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_flag = KIR_civil_war_meltdown_capital_state_flag
						owner = {
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = KIR_civil_war_meltdown_capital_state_flag
						owner = {
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 1 }
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = owner
						}
						to_state_array = owner.controlled_states
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KAB
						count = KAB.KIR_preCWII_democratic_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KWF
						count = KWF.KIR_preCWII_neutrality_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KRS
						count = KRS.KIR_preCWII_communism_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_state = {
						has_state_flag = KIR_civil_war_meltdown_capital_state_flag
						owner = {
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states < 2 }
						}
					}
				}
				1059 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KAB
						count = KAB.KIR_preCWII_democratic_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KWF
						count = KWF.KIR_preCWII_neutrality_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Nirik Band\" start_equipment_factor = 0.9 start_experience_factor = 0.25"
						owner = KRS
						count = KRS.KIR_preCWII_communism_popularity_var
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			KIS = {
				set_technology = {
					popup = no
					KIR_militia_tech = 1
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army"
					template_counter = 83
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
					support = {
						artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"'Princess Fall Shade' Anti-Nirik Patriotic Regiment\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.8 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"No. 2 Anti-Nirik Patriotic Army 'Save the Realm'\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.8 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"All-Kiria Business and Trade Circles Patriotic Salvation Roundtable Volunteer Brigade\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.6 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"No. 3 Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army 'Fragrancese Volunteer Rifles'\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.6 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"No. 5 Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.5 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"No. 6 Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\" division_template = \"Anti-Nirik Mutual Protection Army\"  start_equipment_factor = 0.5 start_experience_factor = 0.1"
						owner = KIS
						count = 1
					}

		}

			has_completed_focus = KIR_TRAD_4
			has_completed_focus = KIR_TRAD_4_X
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = KIR_unlock_post_war_focus_tree
			days > 480
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.50.a
		country_event = { id = kirin_loyalists.51 hours = 36 }
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.50.b
		country_event = { id = kirin_loyalists.52 hours = 36 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_loyalists.53
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_loyalists.53"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = KIR_TRAD_hierocrat_assassinated days = 30 value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { all_hchs_array^num = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { KIR_hch_to_kill = all_hchs_array^0 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { KIR_total_num_of_hchs = all_hchs_array^num }
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = KIR_random_hch_num
					max = KIR_total_num_of_hchs
					min = 0
					integer = yes
				}
				set_variable = { KIR_hch_to_kill = all_hchs_array^KIR_random_hch_num }
				clear_variable = KIR_total_num_of_hchs
				clear_variable = KIR_random_hch_num
			}
			## Kill HCH
			remove_from_array = { all_hchs_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { kir_hchs_level_1_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
				}
				remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_1_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
				subtract_from_variable = { kir_hchs_level_1_promoted = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { kir_hchs_level_2_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
				}
				remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_2_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
				subtract_from_variable = { kir_hchs_level_2_promoted = 1 }
			}
			remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_3_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
			remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_4_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
			remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_5_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
		}
	}

	title = kirin_loyalists.53.t
	desc = kirin_loyalists.53.d
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_street

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIR
		check_variable = { all_hchs_array^num > 0 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KIR_TRAD_new_standard_army_revolt }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = KIR_TRAD_hierocrat_assassinated }
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = KIR_TRAD_4
			has_completed_focus = KIR_TRAD_4_X
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = KIR_unlock_post_war_focus_tree
			days > 240
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_tech = tech_kirin_astrology
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.53.a
		clear_variable = KIR_hch_to_kill
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_loyalists_assassination_tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_loyalists.59
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_loyalists.59"}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { ## Happens once to either KIR or NSA depending who the player is in charge of. If the player is in charge of neither then it won't matter anyway.
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				KIR = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { all_hchs_array^num = 1 }
						}
						set_variable = { KIR_hch_to_kill = all_hchs_array^0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_variable = { KIR_total_num_of_hchs = all_hchs_array^num }
						set_variable_to_random = {
							var = KIR_random_hch_num
							max = KIR_total_num_of_hchs
							min = 0
							integer = yes
						}
						set_variable = { KIR_hch_to_kill = all_hchs_array^KIR_random_hch_num }
						clear_variable = KIR_total_num_of_hchs
						clear_variable = KIR_random_hch_num
					}
					## Kill HCH
					remove_from_array = { all_hchs_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { kir_hchs_level_1_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
						}
						remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_1_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
						subtract_from_variable = { kir_hchs_level_1_promoted = 1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { kir_hchs_level_2_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
						}
						remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_2_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
						subtract_from_variable = { kir_hchs_level_2_promoted = 1 }
					}
					remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_3_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
					remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_4_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
					remove_from_array = { kir_hchs_level_5_array = KIR_hch_to_kill }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	title = kirin_loyalists.59.t
	desc = kirin_loyalists.59.d
	picture = GFX_event_KIR_cityfall

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.59.a
		trigger = {
			tag = KIR
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			clear_variable = KIR_hch_to_kill
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -25
		KIR = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_loyalists_assassination_tt
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin_loyalists.59.b
		trigger = {
			tag = NSA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			clear_variable = KIR_hch_to_kill
		}
		add_political_power = 75
		KIR = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_loyalists_assassination_tt
		}
	}

		}
		transfer_state = 1061
		1061 = {
			add_core_of = KIS
			remove_core_of = KIR
		}
		transfer_state = 1066
		1066 = {
			add_core_of = KIS
			remove_core_of = KIR
		}
		transfer_state = 1070
		1070 = {
			add_core_of = KIS
			remove_core_of = KIR
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = KIR
					original_tag = KIC
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = kirin_news.3 hours = 12 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_fickle_current
		set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_protag = 3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_council_chose_peaceful_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_entry = 4 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_council_chose_war_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_entry = 5 }
		}
		KIR_diary_add_entry_to_protagonist = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.18.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_KIS_chose_option_reject_outcome
				NOT = { has_country_flag = KIR_KIS_chose_option_respect_outcome }
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = KIS.KIS_plebiscite_average_popular_support ##total failure
				value = 65
				compare = less_than
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = KIS_northern_compact_plebiscite_ongoing_flag
		add_political_power = -300
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = KIR
					original_tag = KIC
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = kirin_news.4 hours = 12 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_unlock_entry_fickle_current
		set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_protag = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_KIR_diary_entry = 6 }
		KIR_diary_add_entry_to_protagonist = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_council.18.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_KIS_chose_option_reject_outcome
				NOT = { has_country_flag = KIR_KIS_chose_option_respect_outcome }
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = KIS.KIS_plebiscite_average_popular_support
				value = 80
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = KIS.KIS_plebiscite_average_popular_support ##CONTESTED OUTCOME

				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}

				}

					type = arms_factory
					level = KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_mil_level

				}

					}

			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1059_mil_level = 1 }
			}
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level > 0 }
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIS
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex

						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { KIS.KIR_loot_cities_1073_civ_level = 1 }

				}
			}
			CFR_steal_diary_KIC = yes
			set_country_flag = CFR_stole_KIC_journal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KIR = {
					exists = yes
					controls_state = 1059
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				CFR_steal_diary_KIR_AB = yes
				set_country_flag = CFR_stole_KIR_AB_journal
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				CFR_steal_diary_KIR_WF = yes
				set_country_flag = CFR_stole_KIR_WF_journal
			}
		}
		set_variable = { var = KIR_diary_SG_trigger_button_offset_X value = -47 }
		set_variable = { var = KIR_diary_SG_glowy_shiny_sparkly_glimmery_shimmery_thing_offset_X value = -89 }
		set_variable = { var = KIR_diary_SG_new_entry_notification_offset_X value = -117 }
		set_variable = { var = KIR_diary_SG_glowy_shiny_sparkly_glimmery_shimmery_thing_offset_Y value = -30 }
		set_variable = { var = KIR_diary_SG_new_entry_notification_offset_Y value = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_republic.25
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_republic.25"}
	title = kirin_republic.25.t
	desc = kirin_republic.25.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_evening

	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIC
		controls_state = 1077
		has_war_with = KIR
		KIR = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = KIR_focus_4e
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_fickle_current_rejected_roaring_fire_flag
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_fickle_current_allied_roaring_fire_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin_republic.25.a
		country_event = { id = kirin_republic.26 days = 7 }
	}
}

						desc = "KIR_rising_sun_desc"

				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}

					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.5

					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = KIR_communism_party_5_long

	}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_republic.31
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_republic.31"}
	title = kirin_republic.31.t
	desc = kirin_republic.31.d

	picture = GFX_event_KIR_street
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KIC
		exists = yes
		has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
		KIR_controls_all_kiria_proper = yes
		KIR = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = KIC
				has_country_flag = KIR_CIVIL_WAR_SCRIPTED_GAME_RULE_TIMER
			}
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
		KIS = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = KIC
			}
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = kirin_republic.31.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_republic_31_tt
		set_country_flag = KIC_unlock_postwar_focus_tree
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIC_fled_to_taungpau
			}
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.25
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = "KIR_rising_sun"
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "KIR_rising_sun_desc"
					ideology = religious_socialism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { KIR_spiritual_communalist }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = KIR_republic_focus_shared_3
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = KIR_matriarch_protector
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = kirin_utility.53 hours = 8 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				communism < 0.25
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 25
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			load_focus_tree = { tree = KIR_republic_realm_focus_tree keep_completed = yes }
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			KIR = {
				KIR_circuit_board_company = {
					set_nationality = KIC
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = KIR_circuit_board_company_available
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = 25000 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_line_break
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
		show_ideas_tooltip = KIR_aureolin_monastery
		set_country_flag = KIR_aureolin_monastery_available
	}
}

			declare_war_on = {
				target = FRV
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
		NRM = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FRV
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				EQS = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = EQS
				save_event_target_as = KIR_EQS
				set_country_flag = KIR_EQS
				EQS = { PREV = { transfer_technology = yes } }
				##States
				transfer_state = 833
				set_capital = {
					state = 833
				}
				##Cores
				EQS = {
					every_core_state = {
						remove_core_of = EQS
					}
				}
				833 = {
					add_core_of = HSZ
				}
				##Cosmetic Tag
				set_cosmetic_tag = KIR_EQS
				##Politics
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 30
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = KIR_EQS_party_long
					name = KIR_EQS_party
				}
				EQS = {
					give_guarantee = PREV
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = KIR
							original_tag = KIS
							tag = SGM
							tag = FRV
						}
						NOT = {
							tag = KRF
						}
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = PREV
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
				##Leader
				KIR = { KIR_EQS_mare = {
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				} }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = "KIR_EQS_mare"
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = harmonic_libertarianism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { }
					}
				}
				##Other
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = { division = "name = \"Hyacinth Volunteer Force\" division_template = \"Militiakirin Brigade\" start_equipment_factor = 1 start_experience_factor = 0.25" owner = PREV }
				}
				add_ideas = KIR_fail_state_refugees
				load_focus_tree = blank_focus_tree
				reserve_dynamic_country = yes
				set_AI_strategies_on_every_possible_country_delayed = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				#HSZ = {
				#	exists = no
				#}
				EQS = {
					OR = {
						exists = no

					}
				}

				}
			}
			add_ideas = KIR_fail_state_hell

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kirin_test.6 ##Randomise Banner Configuration
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event kirin_test.6"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ROOT.controlled_states
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = FlagCoreVarRandom
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 6
			}
			round_temp_variable = FlagCoreVarRandom
			set_variable = { FlagCoreVar = FlagCoreVarRandom }
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = FlagBorderVarRandom
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 10
			}
			round_temp_variable = FlagBorderVarRandom
			set_variable = { FlagBorderVar = FlagBorderVarRandom }
		}
	}
}

				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_CIVIL_WAR_MANUAL_TRIGGER
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin.101 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin_setup.14 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_setup.13.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_available
				set_country_flag = KIR_pol_3_available
				set_country_flag = KIR_great_leap_begun
				complete_national_focus = KIR_focus_2a
				complete_national_focus = KIR_focus_2b
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_CIVIL_WAR_MANUAL_TRIGGER
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin.101 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_expelled_communists
			}
			country_event = { id = kirin_setup.14 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kirin_setup.13.e
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_did_not_expel_communists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = KIR_pol_1_available

				set_country_flag = KIR_PATH_CIVIL_WAR_MANUAL_TRIGGER
			}
